msg:Chongqing Huachen International Hotel is the most cost-effective five-star hotel in Yubei
I recommend the most cost-effective hotel in Yubei to everyone. It covers the unique mountains and cities of Chongqing. Enjoy all the visual feasts and you will never be disappointed.
About the stay experience
The first feeling after staying is that the hotel's location is great. It is only 3 kilometers away from Chongqing Jiangbei Airport. It is separated by a mountain. You can get to the hotel through the tunnel. It takes only 10 minutes to take a taxi. It is a few kilometers away from the airport, but there is no noise and no sound of airplanes. The higher the floor, the better the vision. There is a wetland park opposite, which is worth visiting. It is only 100 meters away from the hotel. There is a mountain city trail Guanyinyan Park on the back mountain. It is a great hotel for leisure and sleep. There is also the Chongqing Yubei Gymnasium diagonally opposite. It is often difficult to book a hotel when there are performances and concerts. It is only half an hour's drive to the popular attractions in Yuzhong District. Worth recommending!

posted:Posted April 29, 2023
msg:Although the hotel has been open for ten years, it is still well maintained. The hotel also arranged a car to pick us up this time. The driver was very enthusiastic and answered our questions along the way. It takes fifteen minutes from Jiangbei Airport to the hotel, which is still very fast. This trip coincides with the May Day holiday, so we booked a room in advance. If we booked later, it would be gone. The hotel is listed as a five-star hotel and still has five-star standards. It has all the necessary configurations. The front desk service is very good, and they specially upgraded our room. The view from room 2508 is still very good. There is a small problem with the room, that is, the door of the shower room cannot be closed and water easily overflows. The water pressure is a bit low. I hope the hotel can actively solve it. Bottled water is also placed on the floor for us to take, which is very friendly for us who are traveling. The aunt on the floor is also very polite. Seeing that we brought children, she also gave us an extra set of shower. For toiletries, we asked for ice cubes and scissors at night, which were delivered very quickly. For takeout, you can go downstairs to get it yourself or have the robot deliver it to you, which is very convenient. We didn't experience the swimming pool and fitness this time, because we didn't have so much energy to exercise when we went out to play. Anyway, the stay experience was good and satisfactory. It is rare to have such good service under such a busy situation. I actively recommend this hotel to friends who are getting off the plane or catching a plane. It is also very quiet at night, which is good for sleep quality. It is a little far from the city center, more than 20 kilometers, and the taxi ride is 60 yuan. The hotel breakfast is also very rich. We included two breakfasts, and the children added a breakfast for 24 yuan. The price is very friendly. In short, travel during holidays must be arranged in advance, otherwise it is difficult to book a room. I will pay attention to this hotel next time I come to Chongqing
